SELECT m.ID AS Id,m.PARENT_ID AS ParentId,m.CODE AS Code,m.NAME,m.ICON,m.MODULE_PATH AS ModulePath,m.IS_FUNCTION AS IsFunctionQuery
  FROM SYS_MODULE m
 LEFT JOIN SYS_ROLE_MODULE rm ON rm.MODULE_ID = m.ID
 LEFT JOIN SYS_ROLE_USER ru ON ru.ROLE_ID = rm.ROLE_ID
WHERE (ru.USER_ID = :UserId OR 1=1)
  AND m.ID<>'00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000'
ORDER BY m.CREATE_DATE

-- UserId: '85c63dec-596c-49b4-8d14-12f4c9eaf140' (Type = String, IsNullable = false)

 LEFT JOIN SYS_ROLE_USER ru ON ru.ROLE_ID = rm.ROLE_ID
WHERE (ru.USER_ID = :UserId OR 1=1)
  AND m.ID<>'00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000'

SELECT * 
FROM ( 
SELECT 
"Project1"."C1" AS "C1", 
"Project1"."MigrationId" AS "MigrationId", 
"Project1"."Model" AS "Model", 
"Project1"."ProductVersion" AS "ProductVersion"
FROM ( SELECT 
	"Extent1"."MigrationId" AS "MigrationId", 
	"Extent1"."Model" AS "Model", 
	"Extent1"."ProductVersion" AS "ProductVersion", 
	1 AS "C1"
	FROM "HSL_LOGMANGAGE"."__MigrationHistory" "Extent1"
	WHERE ("Extent1"."ContextKey" = :p__linq__0)
)  "Project1"
ORDER BY "Project1"."MigrationId" DESC
)
WHERE (ROWNUM <= (1) )

SELECT * 
FROM ( 
SELECT 
"Project1"."C1" AS "C1", 
"Project1"."MigrationId" AS "MigrationId", 
"Project1"."Model" AS "Model", 
"Project1"."ProductVersion" AS "ProductVersion"
FROM ( SELECT 
	"Extent1"."MigrationId" AS "MigrationId", 
	"Extent1"."Model" AS "Model", 
	"Extent1"."ProductVersion" AS "ProductVersion", 
	1 AS "C1"
	FROM "HSL_LOGMANGAGE"."__MigrationHistory" "Extent1"
	WHERE ("Extent1"."ContextKey" = :p__linq__0)
)  "Project1"
ORDER BY "Project1"."MigrationId" DESC
)
WHERE (ROWNUM <= (1) )

SELECT * 
FROM ( 
SELECT 
"Project1"."C1" AS "C1", 
"Project1"."MigrationId" AS "MigrationId", 
"Project1"."Model" AS "Model", 
"Project1"."ProductVersion" AS "ProductVersion"
FROM ( SELECT 
	"Extent1"."MigrationId" AS "MigrationId", 
	"Extent1"."Model" AS "Model", 
	"Extent1"."ProductVersion" AS "ProductVersion", 
	1 AS "C1"
	FROM "HSL_LOGMANGAGE"."__MigrationHistory" "Extent1"
	WHERE ("Extent1"."ContextKey" = :p__linq__0)
)  "Project1"
ORDER BY "Project1"."MigrationId" DESC
)
WHERE (ROWNUM <= (1) )

SELECT * 
FROM ( 
SELECT 
"Project1"."C1" AS "C1", 
"Project1"."MigrationId" AS "MigrationId", 
"Project1"."Model" AS "Model", 
"Project1"."ProductVersion" AS "ProductVersion"
FROM ( SELECT 
	"Extent1"."MigrationId" AS "MigrationId", 
	"Extent1"."Model" AS "Model", 
	"Extent1"."ProductVersion" AS "ProductVersion", 
	1 AS "C1"
	FROM "HSL_LOGMANGAGE"."__MigrationHistory" "Extent1"
	WHERE ("Extent1"."ContextKey" = :p__linq__0)
)  "Project1"
ORDER BY "Project1"."MigrationId" DESC
)
WHERE (ROWNUM <= (1) )

 打开了连接
SELECT m.ID AS Id,m.PARENT_ID AS ParentId,m.CODE AS Code,m.NAME,m.ICON,m.MODULE_PATH AS ModulePath,m.IS_FUNCTION AS IsFunctionQuery
  FROM SYS_MODULE m
 LEFT JOIN SYS_ROLE_MODULE rm ON rm.MODULE_ID = m.ID
 LEFT JOIN SYS_ROLE_USER ru ON ru.ROLE_ID = rm.ROLE_ID
WHERE (ru.USER_ID = :UserId OR 1=1)
  AND m.ID<>'00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000'
ORDER BY m.CREATE_DATE

-- UserId: '85c63dec-596c-49b4-8d14-12f4c9eaf140' (Type = String, IsNullable = false)

-- 正在 2019/4/13 17:15:54 +08:00
 执行
-- 已在 0 毫秒内完成，结果为: OracleDataReader

 关闭了连接
